posted:Posted April 7, 2024
msg:I came to Huai'an for the Qingming Festival. I spent a long time choosing on Ctrip and finally booked Jiahua. At that time, I valued the convenient transportation, the rich business district near Wanda, and the service level of a five-star hotel. Overall, I was quite satisfied, but there are some small suggestions as follows, which I suggest the hotel consider:
1. The hotel facilities are relatively old: We are traveling with children, and the children like to watch TV. The TV in the room is really too old, and the sound sounds a bit strange.
2. Poor air conditioning system: In early April, the weather was a little hot, and the hotel air conditioning could not be controlled autonomously. The temperature in the hotel room that day was 26°. The child was too hot, and the waiter was very good. He quickly sent a cold fan, but the cold fan was loud, and the room was very dry. The child had a nosebleed the next morning. It is recommended to release the control of the air conditioner, and please monitor the humidity in the room.
3. The pillow is not very comfortable: This is a matter of opinion. I personally feel that it is not very comfortable and a little low.

Everything else was quite satisfactory. The Chinese restaurant was great. We ordered the 198 set meal for 2 adults and 2 children. It was large and delicious. The soft serve and noodles were very good. A large fruit plate was also given! I only found out that there was a 158 yuan coupon available when I returned to the hotel room. However, the food was still very good. The waitress in the restaurant was also very enthusiastic!

I returned to Huai'an ten years later. Although I saw some bad reviews and Huai'an also opened several more luxurious hotels, I decided to try it again. To be fair, after all, time is here. Some facilities in the hotel are indeed a bit old. This is an objective fact. The maintenance work is 75 points, but Wanda is still my first choice next time I come to Huai'an. Let me talk about the shortcomings first. On the first day of check-in, there was still some obvious dust and hair on the sheets. This really shouldn't be the case. The ventilation system has a bit of cross-smell. I can smell the food in the toilet, which is a bit embarrassing. Hahahaha, there is dust under the light *****. The aunt didn't notice it for 4 days (but this does not hinder the check-in, it's better to wipe it clean). There is also dust in the public areas, such as the cabinet where the telephone is placed in the elevator. There was dust for 4 days (maybe there was a shortage of staff during the Spring Festival). In addition to the dust on the sheets, these are all minor problems. During the stay, it was the Spring Festival. The room attendant wrote a congratulatory note and gave a beautiful candy bag. I like it very much, plus points, I have a healthy I have a habit of using the room card every day. I can enter the gym 24 hours a day by swiping my card, which is a plus. The gym has prepared some disinfectant, hair bands, and disinfectant tissues, which is also very considerate. The breakfast is also very good. After staying for 4 days, the noodle stall aunt remembered that I like to eat noodles, which is also a plus. The toast in the breakfast sandwich is toasted and cut off. It is a product of Hong Kong-style tea restaurant, which is very good. The children eat chocolate cupcakes for every meal. The coffee beans for breakfast are average, they should be dark roasted, and the bitterness is obvious. I don’t like it very much. It is the only flaw. The hot drinks provided include brown sugar ginger tea, which is friendly to women. I like it. The room service is also very fast. Every time I call and need some slippers, they are delivered quickly. The takeaway is also delivered by a robot. The children especially like it. The hotel also provides children’s slippers and toothbrushes and toothpaste for free, which is very good. The hotel’s toiletries are Acca Kappa white moss series, the smell is good, the shampoo and conditioner are comparable to the Kerastase and L'Oreal professional line that I usually use, which is a bit unexpected. In conclusion, during the Spring Festival, in the prime location of Huai'an, more than 500 per night, the shower room is Hansgrohe Wanda Hotel, you deserve it, the price-performance ratio ceiling! ! ! !

Problematic aspects:
1. The complimentary "buffet" for executive rooms booked through the platform for 2 nights or more is actually an administrative courtesy. Since it comes with the executive room, why do we need to emphasize it deliberately? On the day of check-in, I thought it was a complimentary buffet on the first floor, which caused a misunderstanding.
The executive lounges on the 2nd and 18th floors are closed and all have been moved to the Chinese restaurant on the 2nd floor. Since I will be dining out for the next few days, I cannot comment on whether or what form the administrative courtesy is provided. Breakfast is still on the first floor, so if you want executive trea**ent, it is recommended to choose a common room.

To be fair, the Chinese buffet on the day of check-in did not have many varieties, but the taste was still good. But I can’t understand why the emphasis on a service that should be provided becomes value-added.

msg:總體而言，酒店還是不錯的。以下評論四點：
①希望作為高星級酒店，能給客人一份迎賓水果，這不是刻意需要，而是一種禮遇。是差別於其他酒店的服務品質。除此之外，非常滿意。
②酒店的新舊其實並無所謂，衹要整潔乾淨、服務到位就好，這點酒店做的不錯。如果所有的工作人員在與客人面對面擦肩而過的時候，能向去西遊樂園一樣，每個工作人員都能禮貌的打聲招呼，哪怕您好，服務一定會給人留下更深的好印象。
③看了之前其他人員的評論，尤其是那個吐槽把礦泉水放衞生間就抓狂的SH客人，真真覺得搞笑：那個礦泉水本來就是給你刷牙用的。不放衞生間放哪裡？當然，拿來喝也沒毛病。建議酒店放茶台上吧，不然的確左也不是右也不是的感覺。
④吹風機的確low了。該換換了。

3.酒店泳池…你乾脆直接外包出去算了，又臟又小還全都是游泳培訓，澡堂裏面池子沒有水，説是放了水小孩鬧騰得厲害…佩服

msg:本人於2022年5月5號入住該酒店，對於酒店外觀環境來説還是很滿意，其中不滿意地方有如下幾點，第一，不要總是拿防疫做文章，酒店設施設備有問題就抓緊時間維修，空調調到22度製冷，一整個晚上温度都沒有降下來，一直保持在26.5度，壓根兒就沒有降下温度，空調形同虛設，問前台跟客房部就知道拿防疫要求搪塞過去，其二當天晚上在前台預訂早餐，實際並未使用，退房時酒店照樣收取，疫情導致客房入住率不高，大家都能諒解，你在這上面亂收費是什麼道理，吃相真的很難看，還是標榜自己是三星級酒店，最後本人退房時在前台寄存行李一件，與2022年5月6日下午17時左右去前台領取寄存行李，然而抵達貴酒店前台時並未有工作人員在現場值班，叫了很多聲也沒有一個人過來幫忙解決，坐在酒店前台帶門口的貴酒店工作人員一直低頭玩手機，我過去叫她她還是在玩手機也並未幫忙解決問題，一樓餐廳那邊有兩個穿着貴酒店制服的兩個男生在那邊聊天也沒有説過來解決問題，請問這就是貴酒店的服務態度嗎？我就是來取個寄存物品，需要我在前台眼巴巴等半個多小時的時間，這就是貴酒店自詡自己三星級酒店的服務態度，不光吃相難看，連最起碼的服務意識也沒有，我説的這一切有貴酒店前廳一樓內的監控錄像作為證據，麻煩做服務行業就要擺正自己的位置，不要衹是一個外表好看內在空缺的花瓶，連一個快捷酒店都不如，還想再讓人住進去，是不是有點兒痴人説夢。

name:N‍i‍n‍g‍f‍u‍w‍a‍n‍g‍s‍e‍n‍g‍b‍i‍a‍n
info:Grand Deluxe King Room
info:Stayed in October 2021
info:Solo travelers
info:6 Reviews
rating:1.7
posted:Posted October 5, 2021
msg:我很少點評酒店，除非是體驗非常糟糕的情況下才會點評。説以下幾點。
1.當前疫情仍沒結束，又是在國慶旅遊高峯期，這個酒店從頭到尾沒有查過健康碼和行程碼，從頭到尾沒有要求出入人員帶口罩，當天酒店有婚宴，一大幫人沒一個帶口罩的進出酒店乘坐電梯，這一條，我真的應該給你們舉報到防疫部門。
2.第一次給我的房間，裏面有非常嚴重的廚房那種油煙味兒，我有鼻炎，嗅覺本來並不靈敏，但還是聞到了，本來想忍一忍，就住一天，到後來頭實在疼就要求酒店幫我換一下房間。結果給我換了個婚房！床單被套都是大紅色的，嚇不嚇人？酒店客房和前台就這麼不認真？
3.房間裏一個杯子都沒有，不知道是客房忘記放了，還是因為疫情不放，那麼如果因為疫情不放的話，你們連碼都不查了，口罩都不要求帶了，單純的不放杯子是為了省事兒？如果是為了省事兒，那麼一切就説的通了。
4.其他的細節各種問題，客房服務電話的服務人員，明明是接不通前台電話，確騙我説前台説十分鐘後回電。婚宴的賓客吐在了大堂，這點不怪酒店，但過了一個小時還有很嚴重的嘔吐味兒那就是酒店的問題了。
整體不符合五星級酒店標準，細節做的非常非常不到位，就衝著防疫不符合要求，以及極其嚴重的衞生問題，就應該停業整頓。
